Let's make a game!
	name:Wall Destroyer Not So Real Edition
	by:WallKitty
	desc: A rewrite of Wall Destroyer using the new engine that uses ideas from the now-dead project Wall Destroyer Real Edition
	created:04/21/2014
	updated:12/27/2014
	version:4.0

Settings
	building cost increase:110%
	building cost refund:75%
	stylesheet:https://pastebin.com/raw/J1bCRJQB

Buttons
	*hitWall
		on click:yield 1 money
		on click:yield 1 totalMoney
		on click:yield 1 handDamage
		shown
		name:Punch wall
		icon: http://i.imgur.com/108BtPH.png

	*makeBricks
		on click:yield 1 bricks
		on click:yield 1 totalBricks
		on click:yield 1 handBricks
		name:Create Bricks
		icon:http://i.imgur.com/Tdh80P1.png

	*makeBricks2
		on click:yield 1 fourthWallMatter
		on click:yield 1 total4thWallMatter
		on click:yield 1 hand4thWallMatter
		name:Create 4th Wall Bricks
		icon:http://i.imgur.com/TJGos5s.png

	*fastForward
		on click:yield 1 fastForwardRes
		on click:hide fastForward
		on click:show disableFF
		name:Enable Fast Forward (x10 Production Multiplier)

	*disableFF
		on click:lose fastForwardRes
		on click:hide disableFF
		on click:show fastForward
		name:Disable Fast Forward (Removes x10 Production Multiplier)

	*reset
		on click:yield prePrestige prestige
		on click:lose prePrestige
		on click:yield goldBricks timesWon
		on click:lose goldBricks
		on click:yield bonusBossBrick bonusBossPoint
		on click:lose bonusBossBrick

Buildings

	*timeCounter
		on tick:if (resetTimes>=1) yield 0.016666666666666666666666666666 timeSinceReset
		on tick:yield 0.016666666666666666666666666666 timePlayed
		always hidden
		start with:1

	*destroyWall
		desc:"<i>This wall has stood here serving no clear purpose longer than anyone can remember. It's about time someone took the righteous task upon themselves of doing something about it!</i><br> <br>Destroy the wall and move on to a bigger one.<br>Gives <b>25</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>250,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge."
		cost:1000000000 totalMoney
		on earn:yield 2.5e11 money
		on earn:yield 25 bricks
		on earn:yield 25 totalBricks
		passive:grant 1 wallsDestroyed
		passive:grant 1 prePrestige
		name:Destroy wall
		on earn:hide destroyWall
		cost:1 wallRequirement
		on earn:yield 1 wallRequirement
		on earn:show magicUnlock
		on earn:show wallMultiplier
		on earn:show destroyBigWall
		shown
	*destroyBigWall
		desc:"<i>Another, larger wall has reared its useless brick face in the ashes of the first. This one has little minion walls guarding it. We know what we must do.</i><br> <br>Destroy the big 2nd wall and move on to a bigger one.<br>Gives <b>100</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>25,000,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge."
		cost:1e14 totalMoney
		on earn:yield 2.5e13 money
		on earn:yield 100 bricks
		on earn:yield 100 totalBricks
		passive:grant 1 wallsDestroyed
		passive:grant 1 prePrestige
		name:Destroy 2nd wall
		on earn:hide destroyBigWall
		cost:1 wallRequirement
		on earn:yield 1 wallRequirement
		on earn:show magicLevel2
		on earn:show giantUnlock
		on earn:show destroyHugeWall
	*destroyHugeWall
		desc:"<i>Damn, here it is. If we stop now, we won't be proving humankind's unstoppable will!</i><br> <br>Destroy the huge 3rd wall and move on to a bigger one.<br>Gives <b>5,000</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>2,500,000,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>1</b> cosmic knowledge."
		cost:1e16 totalMoney
		on earn:yield 2.5e15 money
		on earn:yield 5000 bricks
		on earn:yield 5000 totalBricks
		passive:grant 1 wallsDestroyed
		passive:grant 1 prePrestige
		name:Destroy 3rd wall
		on earn:hide destroyHugeWall
		cost:1 wallRequirement

		on earn:show magicLevel3
		on earn:show destroyMassiveWall
	*destroyMassiveWall
		desc:"<i>We must continue to press FOURward! FOUR the glory of all who came beFOUR us!</i><br> <br>Destroy the massive 4th wall and move on to the final one.<br>Gives <b>500,000</b> bricks.<br>Awards <b>250,000,000,000,000,000</b> cash.<br>Worth <b>2</b> cosmic knowledge."
		cost:1e18 totalMoney
		on earn:yield 2.5e17 money
		on earn:yield 500000 bricks
		on earn:yield 500000 totalBricks

		passive:grant 2 prePrestige
		name:Destroy 4th wall
